<h3><a id="user-content-class-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#class-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Class 类</h3>
<p>在 Java 中，你每定义一个 java class 实体都会产生一个 Class 对象。也就是说，当我们编写一个类，编译完成后，在生成的 <code>.class</code> 文件中，就会产生一个 Class 对象，这个 Class 对象用于表示这个类的类型信息。Class 中没有公共的构造器，也就是说 Class 对象不能被实例化。下面来简单看一下 Class 类都包括了哪些方法</p>
<p><strong>toString()</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span> toString() {
  <span class="pl-k">return</span> (isInterface() <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>interface <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> (isPrimitive() <span class="pl-k">?</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>class <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>))
    <span class="pl-k">+</span> getName();
}</pre></div>
<p>toString() 方法能够将对象转换为字符串，toString() 首先会判断 Class 类型是否是接口类型，也就是说，普通类和接口都能够用 Class 对象来表示，然后再判断是否是基本数据类型，这里判断的都是基本数据类型和包装类，还有 <code>void </code>类型。</p>
<p>所有的类型如下</p>
<ul>
<li>java.lang.Boolean : 代表 boolean 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Character: 代表 char 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Byte: 代表 byte 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Short: 代表 short 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Integer: 代表 int 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Long: 代表 long 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Float: 代表 float 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Double: 代表 double 数据类型的包装类</li>
<li>java.lang.Void: 代表 void 数据类型的包装类</li>
</ul>
<p>然后是 <code>getName()</code> 方法，这个方法返回类的全限定名称。</p>
<ul>
<li>如果是引用类型，比如 String.class.getName()  -&gt; <code>java.lang.String</code></li>
<li>如果是基本数据类型，byte.class.getName() -&gt; <code>byte</code></li>
<li>如果是数组类型，new Object[3]).getClass().getName() -&gt; <code>[Ljava.lang.Object</code></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>toGenericString()</strong></p>
<p>这个方法会返回类的全限定名称，而且包括类的修饰符和类型参数信息。</p>
<p><strong>forName()</strong></p>
<p>根据类名获得一个 Class 对象的引用，这个方法会使类对象进行初始化。</p>
<p>例如 <code>Class t = Class.forName("java.lang.Thread")</code> 就能够初始化一个 Thread 线程对象</p>
<p>在 Java 中，一共有三种获取类实例的方式</p>
<ul>
<li>Class.forName(java.lang.Thread)</li>
<li>Thread.class</li>
<li>thread.getClass()</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>newInstance()</strong></p>
<p>创建一个类的实例，代表着这个类的对象。上面 forName() 方法对类进行初始化，newInstance 方法对类进行实例化。</p>
<p><strong>getClassLoader()</strong></p>
<p>获取类加载器对象。</p>
<p><strong>getTypeParameters()</strong></p>
<p>按照声明的顺序获取对象的参数类型信息。</p>
<p><strong>getPackage()</strong></p>
<p>返回类的包</p>
<p><strong>getInterfaces()</strong></p>
<p>获得当前类实现的类或是接口，可能是有多个，所以返回的是 Class 数组。</p>
<p><strong>Cast</strong></p>
<p>把对象转换成代表类或是接口的对象</p>
<p><strong>asSubclass(Class clazz)</strong></p>
<p>把传递的类的对象转换成代表其子类的对象</p>
<p><strong>getClasses()</strong></p>
<p>返回一个数组，数组中包含该类中所有公共类和接口类的对象</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredClasses()</strong></p>
<p>返回一个数组，数组中包含该类中所有类和接口类的对象</p>
<p><strong>getSimpleName()</strong></p>
<p>获得类的名字</p>
<p><strong>getFields()</strong></p>
<p>获得所有公有的属性对象</p>
<p><strong>getField(String name)</strong></p>
<p>获得某个公有的属性对象</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredField(String name)</strong></p>
<p>获得某个属性对象</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredFields()</strong></p>
<p>获得所有属性对象</p>
<p><strong>getAnnotation(Class annotationClass)</strong></p>
<p>返回该类中与参数类型匹配的公有注解对象</p>
<p><strong>getAnnotations()</strong></p>
<p>返回该类所有的公有注解对象</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredAnnotation(Class annotationClass)</strong></p>
<p>返回该类中与参数类型匹配的所有注解对象</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredAnnotations()</strong></p>
<p>返回该类所有的注解对象</p>
<p><strong>getConstructor(Class...&lt;?&gt; parameterTypes)</strong></p>
<p>获得该类中与参数类型匹配的公有构造方法</p>
<p><strong>getConstructors()</strong></p>
<p>获得该类的所有公有构造方法</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredConstructor(Class...&lt;?&gt; parameterTypes)</strong></p>
<p>获得该类中与参数类型匹配的构造方法</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredConstructors()</strong></p>
<p>获得该类所有构造方法</p>
<p><strong>getMethod(String name, Class...&lt;?&gt; parameterTypes)</strong></p>
<p>获得该类某个公有的方法</p>
<p><strong>getMethods()</strong></p>
<p>获得该类所有公有的方法</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredMethod(String name, Class...&lt;?&gt; parameterTypes)</strong></p>
<p>获得该类某个方法</p>
<p><strong>getDeclaredMethods()</strong></p>
<p>获得该类所有方法</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-field-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#field-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Field 类</h3>
<p>Field 类提供类或接口中单独字段的信息，以及对单独字段的动态访问。</p>
<p>这里就不再对具体的方法进行介绍了，读者有兴趣可以参考官方 API</p>
<p>这里只介绍几个常用的方法</p>
<p><strong>equals(Object obj)</strong></p>
<p>属性与obj相等则返回true</p>
<p><strong>get(Object obj)</strong></p>
<p>获得obj中对应的属性值</p>
<p><strong>set(Object obj, Object value)</strong></p>
<p>设置obj中对应属性值</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-method-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#method-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Method 类</h3>
<p><strong>invoke(Object obj, Object... args)</strong></p>
<p>传递object对象及参数调用该对象对应的方法</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-classloader-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#classloader-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ClassLoader 类</h3>
<p>反射中，还有一个非常重要的类就是 ClassLoader 类，类装载器是用来把<code>类(class)</code> 装载进 <code>JVM </code>的。ClassLoader 使用的是双亲委托模型来搜索加载类的，这个模型也就是双亲委派模型。ClassLoader 的类继承图如下</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/18297231c5c6d8a4a4c0f0563cf46ba5286a0173/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b3065436e2e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/18297231c5c6d8a4a4c0f0563cf46ba5286a0173/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b3065436e2e706e67" alt="YK0eCn.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0eCn.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-枚举" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#枚举"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>枚举</h2>
<p>枚举可能是我们使用次数比较少的特性，在 Java 中，枚举使用 <code>enum</code> 关键字来表示，枚举其实是一项非常有用的特性，你可以把它理解为具有特定性质的类。enum 不仅仅 Java 有，C 和 C++ 也有枚举的概念。下面是一个枚举的例子。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">enum</span> <span class="pl-en">Family</span> {

    <span class="pl-c1">FATHER</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">MOTHER</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">SON</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">Daughter</span>;

}</pre></div>
<p>上面我们创建了一个 <code>Family</code>的枚举类，它具有 4 个值，由于枚举类型都是常量，所以都用大写字母来表示。那么 enum 创建出来了，该如何引用呢？</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">EnumUse</span> {

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
        <span class="pl-smi">Family</span> s <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Family</span><span class="pl-c1"><span class="pl-k">.</span>FATHER</span>;
    }
}</pre></div>
<h3><a id="user-content-枚举特性" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#枚举特性"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>枚举特性</h3>
<p>enum 枚举这个类比较有意思，当你创建完 enum 后，编译器会自动为你的 enum 添加 <code>toString()</code> 方法，能够让你方便的显示 enum 实例的具体名字是什么。除了 toString() 方法外，编译器还会添加 <code>ordinal()</code> 方法，这个方法用来表示 enum 常量的声明顺序，以及 <code>values()</code> 方法显示顺序的值。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> main(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] args) {

  <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-smi">Family</span> family <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">Family</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>values()){
    <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(family <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>, ordinal<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> family<span class="pl-k">.</span>ordinal());
  }
}</pre></div>
<p>enum 可以进行静态导入包，静态导入包可以做到不用输入 <code>枚举类名.常量</code>，可以直接使用常量，神奇吗? 使用 ennum 和 <code>static</code> 关键字可以做到静态导入包</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fafac924ee7c4fcde4e67e2ff89c2229b96d9199/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306d33712e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/fafac924ee7c4fcde4e67e2ff89c2229b96d9199/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306d33712e706e67" alt="YK0m3q.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0m3q.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1ef72c53b24d2cf70316a84ebb0f4ac75e6aefe8/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306e67302e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1ef72c53b24d2cf70316a84ebb0f4ac75e6aefe8/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306e67302e706e67" alt="YK0ng0.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0ng0.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>上面代码导入的是 Family 中所有的常量，也可以单独指定常量。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-枚举和普通类一样" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#枚举和普通类一样"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>枚举和普通类一样</h3>
<p>枚举就和普通类一样，除了枚举中能够方便快捷的定义<code>常量</code>，我们日常开发使用的 <code>public static final xxx</code> 其实都可以用枚举来定义。在枚举中也能够定义属性和方法，千万不要把它看作是异类，它和万千的类一样。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">enum</span> <span class="pl-en">OrdinalEnum</span> {

    <span class="pl-c1">WEST</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>live in west<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
    <span class="pl-c1">EAST</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>live in east<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
    <span class="pl-c1">SOUTH</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>live in south<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>),
    <span class="pl-c1">NORTH</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>live in north<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);

    <span class="pl-smi">String</span> description;

    <span class="pl-en">OrdinalEnum</span>(<span class="pl-smi">String</span> <span class="pl-v">description</span>){
        <span class="pl-c1">this</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>description <span class="pl-k">=</span> description;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span> <span class="pl-en">getDescription</span>() {
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> description;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">setDescription</span>(<span class="pl-smi">String</span> <span class="pl-v">description</span>) {
        <span class="pl-c1">this</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>description <span class="pl-k">=</span> description;
    }

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
        <span class="pl-k">for</span>(<span class="pl-smi">OrdinalEnum</span> ordinalEnum <span class="pl-k">:</span> <span class="pl-smi">OrdinalEnum</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>values()){
            <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(ordinalEnum<span class="pl-k">.</span>getDescription());
        }
    }
}</pre></div>
<p>一般 switch 可以和 enum 一起连用，来构造一个小型的状态转换机。</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">enum</span> <span class="pl-en">Signal</span> {
  <span class="pl-c1">GREEN</span>, <span class="pl-c1">YELLOW</span>, <span class="pl-c1">RED</span>
}

<span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">TrafficLight</span> {
    <span class="pl-smi">Signal</span> color <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Signal</span><span class="pl-c1"><span class="pl-k">.</span>RED</span>;

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">change</span>() {
        <span class="pl-k">switch</span> (color) {
        <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">RED</span><span class="pl-k">:</span>
            color <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Signal</span><span class="pl-c1"><span class="pl-k">.</span>GREEN</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
        <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">YELLOW</span><span class="pl-k">:</span>
            color <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Signal</span><span class="pl-c1"><span class="pl-k">.</span>RED</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
        <span class="pl-k">case</span> <span class="pl-c1">GREEN</span><span class="pl-k">:</span>
            color <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">Signal</span><span class="pl-c1"><span class="pl-k">.</span>YELLOW</span>;
            <span class="pl-k">break</span>;
        }
    }
}</pre></div>
<p>是不是代码顿时觉得优雅整洁了些许呢？</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-枚举神秘之处" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#枚举神秘之处"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>枚举神秘之处</h3>
<p>在 Java 中，万事万物都是对象，enum 虽然是个关键字，但是它却隐式的继承于 <code>Enum</code> 类。我们来看一下 Enum 类，此类位于 <code>java.lang</code> 包下，可以自动引用。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1ef72c53b24d2cf70316a84ebb0f4ac75e6aefe8/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306e67302e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1ef72c53b24d2cf70316a84ebb0f4ac75e6aefe8/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306e67302e706e67" alt="YK0ng0.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0ng0.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>此类的属性和方法都比较少。你会发现这个类中没有我们的 values 方法。前面刚说到，<code>values()</code> 方法是你使用枚举时被编译器添加进来的 static 方法。<strong>可以使用反射来验证一下</strong>。</p>
<p>除此之外，enum 还和 Class 类有交集，在 Class 类中有三个关于 Enum 的方法</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/61a2ca68b269141e94697cf7664f7ecdbf18f2d2/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b307576562e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/61a2ca68b269141e94697cf7664f7ecdbf18f2d2/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b307576562e706e67" alt="YK0uvV.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0uvV.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>前面两个方法用于获取 enum 常量，<code>isEnum</code> 用于判断是否是枚举类型的。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-枚举类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#枚举类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>枚举类</h3>
<p>除了 Enum 外，还需要知道两个关于枚举的工具类，一个是 <code>EnumSet</code> ，一个是 <code>EnumMap</code></p>
<p><strong>EnumSet 和 EnumMap</strong></p>
<p>EnumSet 是 JDK1.5 引入的，EnumSet 的设计充分考虑到了速度因素，使用 EnumSet 可以作为 Enum 的替代者，因为它的效率比较高。</p>
<p>EnumMap 是一种特殊的 Map，它要求其中的 key 键值是来自一个 enum。因为 EnumMap 速度也很快，我们可以使用 EnumMap 作为 key 的快速查找。</p>
<p>总的来说，枚举的使用不是很复杂，它也是 Java 中很小的一块功能，但有时却能够因为这一个小技巧，能够让你的代码变得优雅和整洁。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-io" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#io"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>I/O</h2>
<p>创建一个良好的 I/O 程序是非常复杂的。JDK 开发人员编写了大量的类只为了能够创建一个良好的工具包，想必编写 I/O 工具包很费劲吧。</p>
<p>IO 类设计出来，肯定是为了解决 IO 相关操作的，最常见的 I/O 读写就是网络、磁盘等。在 Java 中，对文件的操作是一个典型的 I/O 操作。下面我们就对 I/O 进行一个分类。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a7f4d06f8d028b59ce1c2cf95645d493e89cb8c6/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b304d75542e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a7f4d06f8d028b59ce1c2cf95645d493e89cb8c6/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b304d75542e706e67" alt="YK0MuT.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0MuT.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p>公号回复 <code>IO</code>获取思维导图</p>
</blockquote>
<p>I/O 还可以根据操作对象来进行区分：主要分为</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a85dadd0a62fb518601beda91fa053ab1706bd53/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b305144552e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a85dadd0a62fb518601beda91fa053ab1706bd53/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b305144552e706e67" alt="YK0QDU.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0QDU.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>除此之外，I/O 中还有其他比较重要的类</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-file-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#file-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>File 类</h3>
<p>File 类是对文件系统中文件以及文件夹进行操作的类，可以通过面向对象的思想操作文件和文件夹，是不是很神奇？</p>
<p>文件创建操作如下，主要涉及 <strong>文件创建、删除文件、获取文件描述符等</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">FileDemo</span>{
   <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
       <span class="pl-smi">File</span> file <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>D:<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>file.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
       <span class="pl-k">try</span>{
         f<span class="pl-k">.</span>createNewFile(); <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 创建一个文件</span>
         
         <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> File类的两个常量</span>
         <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>路径分隔符(与系统有关的）&lt;windows里面是 ; linux里面是 ： &gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-smi">File</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>pathSeparator);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>   ;</span>
        <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>与系统有关的路径名称分隔符&lt;windows里面是 \ linux里面是/ &gt;</span>
        <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-smi">File</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>separator);      <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>  \</span>
         
         <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 删除文件</span>
         <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span></span>
<span class="pl-c">         File file = new File(fileName);</span>
<span class="pl-c">         if(f.exists()){</span>
<span class="pl-c">             f.delete();</span>
<span class="pl-c">         }else{</span>
<span class="pl-c">             System.out.println("文件不存在");</span>
<span class="pl-c">         }   </span>
<span class="pl-c">         <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>

         
       }<span class="pl-k">catch</span> (<span class="pl-smi">Exception</span> e) {
           e<span class="pl-k">.</span>printStackTrace();
       }
    }
}</pre></div>
<p>也可以对文件夹进行操作</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">FileDemo</span>{
  <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
    <span class="pl-smi">String</span> fileName <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>D:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>separator <span class="pl-k">+</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>filepackage<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>;
    <span class="pl-smi">File</span> file <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span>(fileName);
    f<span class="pl-k">.</span>mkdir();
    
		<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 列出所有文件</span>
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">/*</span></span>
<span class="pl-c">    String[] str = file.list();</span>
<span class="pl-c">    for (int i = 0; i &lt; str.length; i++) {</span>
<span class="pl-c">      System.out.println(str[i]);</span>
<span class="pl-c">    }</span>
<span class="pl-c">    <span class="pl-c">*/</span></span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 使用 file.listFiles(); 列出所有文件，包括隐藏文件</span>
    
    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> 使用 file.isDirectory() 判断指定路径是否是目录</span>
  }
}</pre></div>
<p>上面只是举出来了两个简单的示例，实际上，还有一些其他对文件的操作没有使用。比如创建文件，就可以使用三种方式来创建</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre>File(<span class="pl-smi">String</span> directoryPath);
File(<span class="pl-smi">String</span> directoryPath, <span class="pl-smi">String</span> filename);
File(<span class="pl-smi">File</span> dirObj, <span class="pl-smi">String</span> filename);</pre></div>
<p>directoryPath 是文件的路径名，filename 是文件名，dirObj 是一个 File 对象。例如</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-smi">File</span> file <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>D:<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>java<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>file1.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>双\\是转义</span>
<span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(file);
<span class="pl-smi">File</span> file2 <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>D:<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>java<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>file2.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>父路径、子路径--可以适用于多个文件的！</span>
<span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(file2);
<span class="pl-smi">File</span> parent <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span>(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>D:<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>java<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
<span class="pl-smi">File</span> file3 <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-k">new</span> <span class="pl-smi">File</span>(parent,<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>file3.txt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span>File类的父路径、子路径</span>
<span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(file3);</pre></div>
<p>现在对 File 类进行总结</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3508d3fd198a0b25886a9573e18f6f5684ed3464/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306c62462e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3508d3fd198a0b25886a9573e18f6f5684ed3464/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b306c62462e706e67" alt="YK0lbF.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0lbF.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-基础-io-类和相关方法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#基础-io-类和相关方法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>基础 IO 类和相关方法</h3>
<p>虽然. IO 类有很多，但是最基本的是四个抽象类，<strong>InputStream、OutputStream、Reader、Writer</strong>。最基本的方法也就是 <code>read()</code> 和 <code>write()</code> 方法，其他流都是上面这四类流的子类，方法也是通过这两类方法衍生而成的。而且大部分的 IO 源码都是 <code>native</code> 标志的，也就是说源码都是 C/C++ 写的。这里我们先来认识一下这些流类及其方法</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-inputstream" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#inputstream"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>InputStream</h4>
<p>InputStream 是一个定义了 Java 流式字节输入模式的抽象类。该类的所有方法在出错条件下引发一个IOException 异常。它的主要方法定义如下</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3d49898e68ee260deab36906ba9170c2dcfeed02/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b303345342e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3d49898e68ee260deab36906ba9170c2dcfeed02/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b303345342e706e67" alt="YK03E4.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK03E4.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-outputstream" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#outputstream"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>OutputStream</h4>
<p>OutputStream 是定义了流式字节输出模式的抽象类。该类的所有方法返回一个void 值并且在出错情况下引发一个IOException异常。它的主要方法定义如下</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/99f6e1049a7573f9c181f5d903d805a51bc8bdc7/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b3038554a2e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/99f6e1049a7573f9c181f5d903d805a51bc8bdc7/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b3038554a2e706e67" alt="YK08UJ.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK08UJ.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-reader-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#reader-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Reader 类</h4>
<p>Reader 是 Java 定义的流式字符输入模式的抽象类。类中的方法在出错时引发 <code>IOException</code> 异常。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2891959ca027e0f792a77c122da734bc30054df4/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b305943522e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2891959ca027e0f792a77c122da734bc30054df4/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b305943522e706e67" alt="YK0YCR.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0YCR.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-writer-类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#writer-类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Writer 类</h4>
<p>Writer 是定义流式字符输出的抽象类。 所有该类的方法都返回一个 void 值并在出错条件下引发 IOException 异常</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1fdc3ad59c081d72a545db252d95cc4e8ee6e674/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b307438312e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/1fdc3ad59c081d72a545db252d95cc4e8ee6e674/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b307438312e706e67" alt="YK0t81.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0t81.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-inputstream-及其子类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#inputstream-及其子类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>InputStream 及其子类</h3>
<p><strong>FileInputStream 文件输入流</strong>： FileInputStream 类创建一个能从文件读取字节的 InputStream 类</p>
<p><strong>ByteArrayInputStream 字节数组输入流</strong> ： 把内存中的一个缓冲区作为 InputStream 使用</p>
<p><strong>PipedInputStream 管道输入流</strong>： 实现了pipe 管道的概念，主要在线程中使用</p>
<p><strong>SequenceInputStream 顺序输入流</strong>：把多个 InputStream 合并为一个 InputStream</p>
<p><strong>FilterOutputStream 过滤输入流</strong>：其他输入流的包装。</p>
<p><strong>ObjectInputStream 反序列化输入流</strong> ： 将之前使用 ObjectOutputStream 序列化的原始数据恢复为对象，以流的方式读取对象</p>
<p>**DataInputStream ** : 数据输入流允许应用程序以与机器无关方式从底层输入流中读取基本 Java 数据类型。</p>
<p><strong>PushbackInputStream 推回输入流</strong>： 缓冲的一个新颖的用法是实现<code>推回 （pushback）</code> 。 Pushback 用于输入流允许字节被读取然后返回到流。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-outputstream-及其子类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#outputstream-及其子类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>OutputStream 及其子类</h3>
<p><strong>FileOutputStream 文件输出流</strong>： 该类实现了一个输出流，其数据写入文件。</p>
<p><strong>ByteArrayOutputStream 字节数组输出流</strong> ：该类实现了一个输出流，其数据被写入由 byte 数组充当的缓冲区，缓冲区会随着数据的不断写入而自动增长。</p>
<p><strong>PipedOutputStream 管道输出流</strong> ：管道的输出流，是管道的发送端。</p>
<p><strong>ObjectOutputStream 基本类型输出流</strong>  ：该类将实现了序列化的对象序列化后写入指定地方。</p>
<p><strong>FilterOutputStream 过滤输出流</strong>：其他输出流的包装。</p>
<p><strong>PrintStream 打印流</strong> 通过 PrintStream 可以将文字打印到文件或者网络中去。</p>
<p>**DataOutputStream ** : 数据输出流允许应用程序以与机器无关方式向底层输出流中写入基本 Java 数据类型。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-reader-及其子类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#reader-及其子类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Reader 及其子类</h3>
<p><strong>FileReader 文件字符输入流</strong> ： 把文件转换为字符流读入</p>
<p><strong>CharArrayReader 字符数组输入流</strong> ： 是一个把字符数组作为源的输入流的实现</p>
<p><strong>BufferedReader 缓冲区输入流</strong> ： BufferedReader 类从字符输入流中读取文本并缓冲字符，以便有效地读取字符，数组和行</p>
<p>**PushbackReader **: PushbackReader 类允许一个或多个字符被送回输入流。</p>
<p><strong>PipedReader 管道输入流</strong>： 主要用途也是在线程间通讯，不过这个可以用来传输字符</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-writer-及其子类" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#writer-及其子类"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Writer 及其子类</h3>
<p><strong>FileWriter 字符输出流</strong> ： FileWriter 创建一个可以写文件的 Writer 类。</p>
<p><strong>CharArrayWriter 字符数组输出流</strong>： CharArrayWriter 实现了以数组作为目标的输出流。</p>
<p><strong>BufferedWriter 缓冲区输出流</strong> ： BufferedWriter是一个增加了<code>flush( )</code> 方法的Writer。 flush( )方法可以用来确保数据缓冲器确实被写到实际的输出流。</p>
<p>**PrintWriter ** ： PrintWriter 本质上是 PrintStream 的字符形式的版本。</p>
<p><strong>PipedWriter 管道输出流</strong>： 主要用途也是在线程间通讯，不过这个可以用来传输字符</p>
<p>Java 的输入输出的流式接口为复杂而繁重的任务提供了一个简洁的抽象。过滤流类的组合允许你动态建立客户端流式接口来配合数据传输要求。继承高级流类 InputStream、InputStreamReader、 Reader 和 Writer 类的 Java 程序在将来 （即使创建了新的和改进的具体类）也能得到合理运用。</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-注解" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#注解"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>注解</h2>
<p>Java <code>注解（Annotation）</code> 又称为<code>元数据</code> ，它为我们在代码中添加信息提供了一种形式化的方法。它是 JDK1.5 引入的，Java 定义了一套注解，共有 7 个，3 个在 <code>java.lang</code> 中，剩下 4 个在 <code>java.lang.annotation</code> 中。</p>
<p>作用在代码中的注解有三个，它们分别是</p>
<ul>
<li><code>@Override</code>： 重写标记，一般用在子类继承父类后，标注在重写过后的子类方法上。如果发现其父类，或者是引用的接口中并没有该方法时，会报编译错误。</li>
<li><code>@Deprecated</code> ：用此注解注释的代码已经过时，不再推荐使用</li>
<li><code>@SuppressWarnings</code>： 这个注解起到忽略编译器的警告作用</li>
</ul>
<p>元注解有四个，元注解就是用来标志注解的注解。它们分别是</p>
<ul>
<li><code>@Retention</code>: 标识如何存储，是只在代码中，还是编入class文件中，或者是在运行时可以通过反射访问。</li>
</ul>
<p>RetentionPolicy.SOURCE：注解只保留在源文件，当 Java 文件编译成class文件的时候，注解被遗弃；</p>
<p>RetentionPolicy.CLASS：注解被保留到 class 文件，但 jvm 加载 class 文件时候被遗弃，这是<code>默认的</code>生命周期；</p>
<p>RetentionPolicy.RUNTIME：注解不仅被保存到 class 文件中，jvm 加载 class 文件之后，仍然存在；</p>
<ul>
<li><code>@Documented</code>: 标记这些注解是否包含在 JavaDoc 中。</li>
<li><code>@Target</code>： 标记这个注解说明了 Annotation 所修饰的对象范围，Annotation 可被用于 packages、types（类、接口、枚举、Annotation类型）、类型成员（方法、构造方法、成员变量、枚举值）、方法参数和本地变量（如循环变量、catch参数）。取值如下</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">enum</span> <span class="pl-en">ElementType</span> {
    <span class="pl-c1">TYPE</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">FIELD</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">METHOD</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">PARAMETER</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">CONSTRUCTOR</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">LOCAL_VARIABLE</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">ANNOTATION_TYPE</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">PACKAGE</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">TYPE_PARAMETER</span>,
    <span class="pl-c1">TYPE_USE</span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>@Inherited</code> ： 标记这个注解是继承于哪个注解类的。</li>
</ul>
<p>从 JDK1.7 开始，又添加了三个额外的注解，它们分别是</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>@SafeVarargs</code> ：在声明可变参数的构造函数或方法时，Java 编译器会报 unchecked 警告。使用 @SafeVarargs 可以忽略这些警告</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>@FunctionalInterface</code>: 表明这个方法是一个函数式接口</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>@Repeatable</code>： 标识某注解可以在同一个声明上使用多次。</p>
</li>
</ul>
<blockquote>
<p>注意：注解是不支持继承的。</p>
</blockquote>
<h2><a id="user-content-关于-null-的几种处理方式" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#关于-null-的几种处理方式"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>关于 null 的几种处理方式</h2>
<p>对于 Java 程序员来说，空指针一直是恼人的问题，我们在开发中经常会受到 NullPointerException 的蹂躏和壁咚。Java 的发明者也承认这是一个巨大的设计错误。</p>
<p>那么关于 null ，你应该知道下面这几件事情来有效的了解 null ，从而避免很多由 null 引起的错误。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/89d73f1a4f15f2ddbf740901d9bf6133d80db894/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b304e67782e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/89d73f1a4f15f2ddbf740901d9bf6133d80db894/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b304e67782e706e67" alt="YK0Ngx.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0Ngx.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-大小写敏感" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#大小写敏感"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>大小写敏感</h3>
<p>首先，null 是 Java 中的<code>关键字</code>，像是 **public、static、final。**它是大小写敏感的，你不能将 null 写成 Null 或 NULL，编辑器将不能识别它们然后报错。</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/be8f59219c73950994c8762254bbdc3f62e43f8b/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b305576362e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/be8f59219c73950994c8762254bbdc3f62e43f8b/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b305576362e706e67" alt="YK0Uv6.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0Uv6.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>这个问题已经几乎不会出现，因为 eclipse 和 Idea 编译器已经给出了编译器提示，所以你不用考虑这个问题。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-null-是任何引用类型的初始值" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#null-是任何引用类型的初始值"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>null 是任何引用类型的初始值</h3>
<p>null 是所有引用类型的默认值，Java 中的任何引用变量都将null作为默认值，也就是说所有 Object 类下的引用类型默认值都是 null。这对所有的引用变量都适用。就像是基本类型的默认值一样，例如 int 的默认值是 0，boolean 的默认值是 false。</p>
<p>下面是基本数据类型的初始值</p>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ab0bfa22ed19cac0632c7333637564b198fddaaf/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b30644b4b2e706e67"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/ab0bfa22ed19cac0632c7333637564b198fddaaf/68747470733a2f2f73312e617831782e636f6d2f323032302f30352f30382f594b30644b4b2e706e67" alt="YK0dKK.png" data-canonical-src="https://s1.ax1x.com/2020/05/08/YK0dKK.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-null-只是一种特殊的值" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#null-只是一种特殊的值"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>null 只是一种特殊的值</h3>
<p>null 既不是对象也不是一种类型，它仅是一种特殊的值，你可以将它赋予任何类型，你可以将 null 转换为任何类型</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> main(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] args) {
  <span class="pl-smi">String</span> str <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;
  <span class="pl-smi">Integer</span> itr <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;
  <span class="pl-smi">Double</span> dou <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;

  <span class="pl-smi">Integer</span> integer <span class="pl-k">=</span> (<span class="pl-smi">Integer</span>) <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;
  <span class="pl-smi">String</span> string <span class="pl-k">=</span> (<span class="pl-smi">String</span>)<span class="pl-c1">null</span>;

  <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>integer = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> integer);
  <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>string = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> string);
}</pre></div>
<p>你可以看到在编译期和运行期内，将 null 转换成任何的引用类型都是可行的，并且不会抛出空指针异常。</p>
<p><strong>null 只能赋值给引用变量，不能赋值给基本类型变量</strong>。</p>
<p><strong>持有 null 的包装类在进行自动拆箱的时候，不能完成转换，会抛出空指针异常，并且 null 也不能和基本数据类型进行对比</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> main(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] args) {
  <span class="pl-k">int</span> i <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>;
  <span class="pl-smi">Integer</span> itr <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;
  <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(itr <span class="pl-k">==</span> i);
}</pre></div>
<p><strong>使用了带有 null 值的引用类型变量，<code>instanceof</code> 操作会返回 false</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> main(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] args) {
  <span class="pl-smi">Integer</span> isNull <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>;
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">//</span> instanceof = isInstance 方法</span>
  <span class="pl-k">if</span>(isNull <span class="pl-k">instanceof</span> <span class="pl-smi">Integer</span>){
    <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>isNull is instanceof Integer<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
  }<span class="pl-k">else</span>{
    <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>isNull is not instanceof Integer<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>);
  }
}</pre></div>
<p>这是 instanceof 操作符一个很重要的特性，使得对类型强制转换检查很有用</p>
<p><strong>静态变量为 null 调用静态方法不会抛出 NullPointerException。因为静态方法使用了静态绑定</strong>。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-使用-null-safe-方法" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#使用-null-safe-方法"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>使用 Null-Safe 方法</h3>
<p>你应该使用 null-safe 安全的方法，java 类库中有很多工具类都提供了静态方法，例如基本数据类型的包装类，Integer , Double 等。例如</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">NullSafeMethod</span> {

    <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span> number;

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
        <span class="pl-smi">String</span> s <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>valueOf(number);
        <span class="pl-smi">String</span> string <span class="pl-k">=</span> number<span class="pl-k">.</span>toString();
        <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>s = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> s);
        <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>string = <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> string);
    }
}</pre></div>
<p>number 没有赋值，所以默认为null，使用<code>String.value(number)</code> 静态方法没有抛出空指针异常，但是使用 <code>toString() </code>却抛出了空指针异常。所以尽量使用对象的静态方法。</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-null-判断" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#null-判断"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>null 判断</h3>
<p>你可以使用 <code>==</code> 或者 <code>!=</code> 操作来比较 null 值，但是不能使用其他算法或者逻辑操作，例如小于或者大于。跟SQL不一样，在Java中 null == null 将返回 true，如下所示：</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-java"><pre><span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-en">CompareNull</span> {

    <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span> str1;
    <span class="pl-k">private</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-smi">String</span> str2;

    <span class="pl-k">public</span> <span class="pl-k">static</span> <span class="pl-k">void</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>(<span class="pl-k">String</span>[] <span class="pl-v">args</span>) {
        <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>str1 == str2 ? <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">+</span> str1 <span class="pl-k">==</span> str2);
        <span class="pl-smi">System</span><span class="pl-k">.</span>out<span class="pl-k">.</span>println(<span class="pl-c1">null</span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">null</span>);
    }
}</pre></div>
<h2><a id="user-content-关于思维导图" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#关于思维导图"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>关于思维导图</h2>
<p>我把一些常用的 Java 工具包的思维导图做了汇总，方便读者查阅。</p>
